I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Public unscoped enum constants not visible across module boundaries
**Issue Description**
After #7798, the constants in public unscoped enums are no longer visible across module boundaries, regardless of `public`.

**Reproducer Code**
```slang
// test_a.slang
[UnscopedEnum]
public enum TestEnum
{
    CASE_A,
    CASE_B
};
```

```slang
// test_b.slang
import test_a;

[numthreads(1, 1, 1)]
void computeMain(int3 dispatchThreadID: SV_DispatchThreadID)
{
    TestEnum e = CASE_A;
}
```

Compile with:
```
slangc -target spirv test_b.slang -o test.spv
```

Error message:
```
test_b.slang(6): error 30600: 'CASE_A' is not accessible from the current context.
    TestEnum e = CASE_A;
```

`TestEnum.CASE_A` is visible and if the enum is moved into `test_b.slang`, the unscoped `CASE_A` is also visible.

**Expected Behavior**
`CASE_A` is visible, as if it was in the same module.

**Actual Behavior**
Error message is given.

**Environment:**
 - Slang Version: a77d22bf3bfc3098b01e4886c3a63fb751edc704
 - OS: OpenSUSE Tumbleweed

**Additional context**
The PR that changed this behaviour is related to issue #7758, where it was mentioned that "canonical Slang code should always use scoped enums." Since modules are a Slang feature, it can also be entirely reasonable to ban unscoped enum visibility across module boundaries.

I have some code that currently uses this feature, but I'm working on moving it to scoped enums, so this issue is not at all a blocker for me. I was more just surprised that there was a change to the exisitng behaviour.

</pr_description>

Can you help me implement the necessary changes to the repository so that the requirements specified in the <pr_description> are met?

+void FacetImpl::init(ASTBuilder* astBuilder)
+{
+    if (directness != Facet::Directness::Self)
+    {
+        // Depending on the type of the facet, we may want to specialize the
+        // declRef that we are going to lookup in. If the facet represents
+        // an extension, we should just lookup in the extension decl.
+        //
+        // If the facet is an extension to an interface type, we should
+        // specialize the interface declRef to the concrete type that this
+        // extension applied to.
+        //
+        // If the facet represents an implementation of interface type,
+        // we should also specialize the interface declRef with the concrete
+        // type info.
+        //
+        declRefForMemberLookup =
+            _maybeSpecializeSuperTypeDeclRef(astBuilder, origin.declRef, getType(), subtypeWitness)
+                .as<ContainerDecl>();
+    }
+    else
+    {
+        declRefForMemberLookup = origin.declRef.as<ContainerDecl>();
+    }
+}

    29	struct BreadcrumbInfo
    30	{
    31	    LookupResultItem::Breadcrumb::Kind kind;
    32	    LookupResultItem::Breadcrumb::ThisParameterMode thisParameterMode =
    33	        LookupResultItem::Breadcrumb::ThisParameterMode::Default;
    34	    DeclRef<Decl> declRef;
    35	    Val* val = nullptr;
    36	    BreadcrumbInfo* prev = nullptr;
    37	};
    38	
    39	//
    40	
    41	bool DeclPassesLookupMask(Decl* decl, LookupMask mask)
    42	{
    43	    // Always exclude extern members from lookup result.
    44	    if (decl->hasModifier<ExtensionExternVarModifier>())
    45	    {
    46	        return false;
    47	    }
    48	    else if (decl->hasModifier<ExternModifier>())
    49	    {
    50	        if (as<ExtensionDecl>(decl->parentDecl))
    51	        {
    52	            return false;
    53	        }
    54	    }
    55	    // type declarations
    56	    if (const auto aggTypeDecl = as<AggTypeDecl>(decl))
    57	    {
    58	        return int(mask) & int(LookupMask::type);
    59	    }
    60	    else if (const auto simpleTypeDecl = as<SimpleTypeDecl>(decl))
    61	    {
    62	        return int(mask) & int(LookupMask::type);
    63	    }
    64	    // function declarations
    65	    else if (const auto funcDecl = as<FunctionDeclBase>(decl))
    66	    {
    67	        return (int(mask) & int(LookupMask::Function)) != 0;
    68	    }
    69	    // attribute declaration
    70	    else if (const auto attrDecl = as<AttributeDecl>(decl))
    71	    {
    72	        return (int(mask) & int(LookupMask::Attribute)) != 0;
    73	    }
    74	    // syntax declaration
    75	    else if (const auto syntaxDecl = as<SyntaxDecl>(decl))
    76	    {
    77	        return (int(mask) & int(LookupMask::SyntaxDecl)) != 0;
    78	    }
    79	    // default behavior is to assume a value declaration
    80	    // (no overloading allowed)
    81	
    82	    return (int(mask) & int(LookupMask::Value)) != 0;
    83	}
    84	
    85	void AddToLookupResult(LookupResult& result, LookupResultItem item)
    86	{
    87	    if (!result.isValid())
    88	    {
    89	        // If we hadn't found a hit before, we have one now
    90	        result.item = item;
    91	    }
    92	    else if (!result.isOverloaded())
    93	    {
    94	        // We are about to make this overloaded
    95	        result.items.add(result.item);
    96	        result.items.add(item);
    97	    }
    98	    else
    99	    {

   240	    }
   241	
   242	    for (Index i = memberCountWhenLastUpdated; i < memberCount; ++i)
   243	    {
   244	        Decl* memberDecl = decls[i];
   245	
   246	        // Transparent member declarations will go into a separate list,
   247	        // so that they can be conveniently queried later for lookup
   248	        // operations.
   249	        //
   250	        // TODO: Rather than track these using a separate table, we
   251	        // could design a scheme where transparent members are put into
   252	        // the same lookup dictionary as everything else, just under
   253	        // a pseudo-name that identifies transparent members.
   254	        //
   255	        if (memberDecl->hasModifier<TransparentModifier>())
   256	        {
   257	            accelerators.filteredListOfTransparentDecls.add(memberDecl);
   258	        }
   259	
   260	        // Members that don't have a name don't go into the lookup dictionary.
   261	        //
   262	        auto memberName = memberDecl->getName();
   263	        if (!memberName)
   264	            continue;
   265	
   266	        // As a special case, we ignore the `inner` member of a
   267	        // `GenericDecl`, since it will always have the same name
   268	        // as the outer generic, and should not be found by lookup.
   269	        //
   270	        // TODO: We really ought to change up our entire encoding
   271	        // of generic declarations in the AST.
   272	        //
   273	        if (genericDecl && memberDecl == genericDecl->inner)
   274	            continue;
   275	
   276	        // It is possible that we have encountered previous declarations
   277	        // that have the same name as `memberDecl`, and in that
   278	        // case we want to wire them up into a singly-linked list.
   279	        //
   280	        // This list makes it easy for a lookup operation to find, e.g.,
   281	        // all of the overloaded functions with a given name.
   282	        //
   283	        Decl* prevMemberWithSameName = nullptr;
   284	        accelerators.mapNameToLastDeclOfThatName.tryGetValue(memberName, prevMemberWithSameName);
   285	        memberDecl->_prevInContainerWithSameName = prevMemberWithSameName;
   286	
   287	        // Whether or not there was a previous declaration with this
   288	        // name, the current `memberDecl` is the last member declaration
   289	        // with that name encountered so far, and it is what we will
   290	        // store in the lookup dictionary.
   291	        //
   292	        accelerators.mapNameToLastDeclOfThatName[memberName] = memberDecl;
   293	    }
   294	
   295	    accelerators.declCountWhenLastUpdated = memberCount;
   296	    SLANG_ASSERT(_areLookupAcceleratorsValid());
   297	}

  4865	static EnumDecl* isUnscopedEnum(Decl* decl)
  4866	{
  4867	    EnumDecl* enumDecl = as<EnumDecl>(decl);
  4868	    if (!enumDecl)
  4869	        return nullptr;
  4870	    for (auto mod : enumDecl->modifiers)
  4871	    {
  4872	        if (as<UnscopedEnumAttribute>(mod))
  4873	        {
  4874	            return enumDecl;
  4875	        }
  4876	        else if (auto uncheckedAttribute = as<UncheckedAttribute>(mod))
  4877	        {
  4878	            // We have to perform an ugly string comparison here, because the attributes
  4879	            // haven't been checked during parsing.
  4880	            if (getText(uncheckedAttribute->keywordName) == "UnscopedEnum")
  4881	            {
  4882	                return enumDecl;
  4883	            }
  4884	        }
  4885	    }
  4886	    return nullptr;
  4887	}

  4891	    Parser* parser,
  4892	    Decl* decl,
  4893	    ContainerDecl* containerDecl,
  4894	    Modifiers modifiers)
  4895	{
  4896	    // Add any modifiers we parsed before the declaration to the list
  4897	    // of modifiers on the declaration itself.
  4898	    //
  4899	    // We need to be careful, because if `decl` is a generic declaration,
  4900	    // then we really want the modifiers to apply to the inner declaration.
  4901	    //
  4902	    Decl* declToModify = decl;
  4903	    if (auto genericDecl = as<GenericDecl>(decl))
  4904	        declToModify = genericDecl->inner;
  4905	
  4906	    if (as<ModuleDeclarationDecl>(decl))

  4909	        auto moduleDecl = getModuleDecl(containerDecl);
  4910	        if (moduleDecl)

   843	static void _lookUpInScopes(
   844	    ASTBuilder* astBuilder,
   845	    Name* name,
   846	    LookupRequest const& request,
   847	    LookupResult& result)
   848	{
   849	    auto thisParameterMode = LookupResultItem::Breadcrumb::ThisParameterMode::Default;
   850	
   851	    auto scope = request.scope;
   852	
   853	    auto endScope = request.endScope;
   854	
   855	    // The file decl that this scope is in.
   856	    FileDecl* thisFileDecl = nullptr;
   857	
   858	    for (; scope != endScope; scope = scope->parent)
   859	    {
   860	        // Note that we consider all "peer" scopes together,
   861	        // so that a hit in one of them does not preclude
   862	        // also finding a hit in another
   863	        for (auto link = scope; link; link = link->nextSibling)
   864	        {
   865	            auto containerDecl = link->containerDecl;
   866	
   867	            // It is possible for the first scope in a list of
   868	            // siblings to be a "dummy" scope that only exists
   869	            // to combine the siblings; in that case it will
   870	            // have a null `containerDecl` and needs to be
   871	            // skipped over.
   872	            //
   873	            if (!containerDecl)
   874	                continue;
   875	
   876	            if (auto fileDecl = as<FileDecl>(containerDecl))
   877	            {
   878	                if (!thisFileDecl)
   879	                    thisFileDecl = fileDecl;
   880	                else if (fileDecl == thisFileDecl)
   881	                {
   882	                    // If we have already looked up in this file decl,
   883	                    // we don't want to do so again.
   884	                    continue;
   885	                }
   886	            }
   887	
   888	            // TODO: If we need default substitutions to be applied to
   889	            // the `containerDecl`, then it might make sense to have
   890	            // each `link` in the scope store a decl-ref instead of
   891	            // just a decl.
   892	            //
   893	            DeclRef<ContainerDecl> containerDeclRef = createDefaultSubstitutionsIfNeeded(
   894	                                                          astBuilder,
   895	                                                          request.semantics,
   896	                                                          makeDeclRef(containerDecl))
   897	                                                          .as<ContainerDecl>();
   898	
   899	            // If the container we are looking into represents a type
   900	            // or an `extension` of a type, then we need to treat
   901	            // this step as lookup into the `this` variable (or the
   902	            // `This` type), which means including any `extension`s
   903	            // or inheritance clauses in the lookup process.
   904	            //
   905	            // Note: The `AggTypeDeclBase` class is the common superclass
   906	            // between `AggTypeDecl` and `ExtensionDecl`.
   907	            //
   908	            if (auto aggTypeDeclBaseRef = containerDeclRef.as<AggTypeDeclBase>())
   909	            {
   910	                // When reconstructing the final expression for a result
   911	                // looked up through the type or extension, we will need
   912	                // a `this` expression (or a `This` type expression) to
   913	                // mark the base of the member reference, so we create
   914	                // a "breadcrumb" here to track that fact.
   915	                //
   916	                BreadcrumbInfo breadcrumb;
   917	                breadcrumb.kind = LookupResultItem::Breadcrumb::Kind::This;
   918	                breadcrumb.thisParameterMode = thisParameterMode;
   919	                breadcrumb.declRef = aggTypeDeclBaseRef;
   920	                breadcrumb.prev = nullptr;

   190	        // If we are looking up for completion suggestions,
   191	        // return all the members that are available.
   192	        for (auto member : containerDecl->getDirectMemberDecls())
   193	        {
   194	            if (!request.shouldConsiderAllLocalNames() && _isUncheckedLocalVar(member))
   195	                continue;
   196	            if (!DeclPassesLookupMask(member, request.mask))
   197	                continue;
   198	            AddToLookupResult(
   199	                result,
   200	                CreateLookupResultItem(
   201	                    astBuilder->getMemberDeclRef<Decl>(parentDeclRef, member),
   202	                    inBreadcrumbs));
   203	        }
   204	    }
   205	    else
   206	    {
   207	        // Iterate over the declarations with the chosen name in the container
   208	        // (if any), and see if we find any that meet our filtering criteria.
   209	        //
   210	        // For example, we might be filtering so that we only consider
   211	        // type declarations.
   212	        //
   213	        for (auto m : containerDecl->getDirectMemberDeclsOfName(name))
   214	        {
   215	            // Skip this declaration if we are checking and this hasn't been
   216	            // checked yet. Because we traverse block statements in order, if
   217	            // it's unchecked or being checked then it isn't declared yet.
   218	            if (!request.shouldConsiderAllLocalNames() && request.semantics &&
   219	                _isUncheckedLocalVar(m))
   220	                continue;
   221	            if (m == request.declToExclude)
   222	                continue;
   223	
   224	            if (!DeclPassesLookupMask(m, request.mask))
   225	                continue;
   226	
   227	            // The declaration passed the test, so add it!
   228	            AddToLookupResult(
   229	                result,
   230	                CreateLookupResultItem(
   231	                    astBuilder->getMemberDeclRef<Decl>(parentDeclRef, m),
   232	                    inBreadcrumbs));
   233	        }
   234	    }
   235	
   236	    // Don't look up transparent members if we are looking for attributes, since
   237	    // they are always defined at global scope in the core module. Trying to lookup transparent
   238	    // members during attribute lookup can lead to infinite recursion on transparent types.
   239	    if ((int)request.mask & (int)LookupMask::Attribute)
   240	        return;
   241	
   242	    // Also skip transparent members if they're explicitly excluded by the
   243	    // request. This prevents cyclic lookups e.g. when looking up UnscopedEnum's
   244	    // underlying types.
   245	    if (((int)request.options & (int)LookupOptions::IgnoreTransparentMembers) != 0)
   246	        return;
   247	
   248	    for (auto transparentMemberDecl : containerDecl->getTransparentDirectMemberDecls())
   249	    {
   250	        // The reference to the transparent member should use the same
   251	        // path as we used in referring to its parent.
   252	        DeclRef<Decl> transparentMemberDeclRef =
   253	            astBuilder->getMemberDeclRef(parentDeclRef, transparentMemberDecl);
   254	        if (transparentMemberDeclRef.getDecl() == request.declToExclude)
   255	            continue;
   256	
   257	        // We need to leave a breadcrumb so that we know that the result
   258	        // of lookup involves a member lookup step here
   259	
   260	        BreadcrumbInfo memberRefBreadcrumb;
   261	        memberRefBreadcrumb.kind = LookupResultItem::Breadcrumb::Kind::Member;
   262	        memberRefBreadcrumb.declRef = transparentMemberDeclRef;
   263	        memberRefBreadcrumb.prev = inBreadcrumbs;
   264	
   265	        _lookUpMembersInValue(
   266	            astBuilder,
   267	            name,
   268	            transparentMemberDeclRef,
   269	            request,
   270	            result,
   271	            &memberRefBreadcrumb);
   272	    }
   273	}
   274	
   275	LookupRequest initLookupRequest(

   800	static void _lookUpMembersInValue(
   801	    ASTBuilder* astBuilder,
   802	    Name* name,
   803	    DeclRef<Decl> valueDeclRef,
   804	    LookupRequest const& request,
   805	    LookupResult& ioResult,
   806	    BreadcrumbInfo* breadcrumbs)
   807	{
   808	    // Looking up `name` in the context of a value can
   809	    // be reduced to the problem of looking up `name`
   810	    // in the *type* of that value.
   811	    //
   812	    auto valueType = getTypeForDeclRef(astBuilder, valueDeclRef, SourceLoc());
   813	    if (auto typeType = as<TypeType>(valueType))
   814	        valueType = typeType->getType();
   815	    return _lookUpMembersInType(astBuilder, name, valueType, request, ioResult, breadcrumbs);
   816	}
   817	
   818	// True if the declaration is of an overloadable variety
   819	// (ie can have multiple definitions with the same name)
   820	//
   821	// For example functions are overloadable, but variables are (typically) not.
   822	static bool _isDeclOverloadable(Decl* decl)
   823	{
   824	    // If it's a generic strip off, to get to inner decl type
   825	    while (auto genericDecl = as<GenericDecl>(decl))
   826	    {
   827	        decl = genericDecl->inner;
   828	    }
   829	
   830	    // TODO(JS): Do we need to special case around ConstructorDecl? or AccessorDecl?
   831	    // It seems not as they are both function-like and potentially overloadable
   832	
   833	    // If it's callable, it's a function-like and so overloadable
   834	    if (auto callableDecl = as<CallableDecl>(decl))
   835	    {
   836	        SLANG_UNUSED(callableDecl);
   837	        return true;
   838	    }
   839	
   840	    return false;
   841	}

   394	static void _lookUpMembersInSuperTypeImpl(
   395	    ASTBuilder* astBuilder,
   396	    Name* name,
   397	    Type* leafType,
   398	    Type* superType,
   399	    SubtypeWitness* leafIsSuperWitness,
   400	    LookupRequest const& request,
   401	    LookupResult& ioResult,
   402	    BreadcrumbInfo* inBreadcrumbs);
   403	
   404	static void _lookUpMembersInSuperType(
   405	    ASTBuilder* astBuilder,
   406	    Name* name,
   407	    Type* leafType,
   408	    Type* superType,
   409	    SubtypeWitness* leafIsSuperWitness,
   410	    LookupRequest const& request,
   411	    LookupResult& ioResult,
   412	    BreadcrumbInfo* inBreadcrumbs)
   413	{
   414	    // If we are looking up through an interface type, then
   415	    // we need to be sure that we add an appropriate
   416	    // "this type" substitution here, since that needs to
   417	    // be applied to any members we look up.
   418	    //
   419	    superType = _maybeSpecializeSuperType(astBuilder, superType, leafIsSuperWitness);
   420	
   421	    // We need to track the indirection we took in lookup,
   422	    // so that we can construct an appropriate AST on the other
   423	    // side that includes the "upcast" from sub-type to super-type.
   424	    //
   425	    BreadcrumbInfo breadcrumb;
   426	    breadcrumb.prev = inBreadcrumbs;
   427	    breadcrumb.kind = LookupResultItem::Breadcrumb::Kind::SuperType;
   428	    breadcrumb.val = leafIsSuperWitness;
   429	    breadcrumb.prev = inBreadcrumbs;
   430	
   431	    _lookUpMembersInSuperTypeImpl(
   432	        astBuilder,
   433	        name,
   434	        leafType,
   435	        superType,
   436	        leafIsSuperWitness,
   437	        request,
   438	        ioResult,
   439	        &breadcrumb);
   440	}
   441	
   442	static void _lookupMembersInSuperTypeFacets(
   443	    ASTBuilder* astBuilder,
   444	    Name* name,
   445	    Type* selfType,
   446	    InheritanceInfo const& inheritanceInfo,
   447	    LookupRequest const& request,
   448	    LookupResult& ioResult,
   449	    BreadcrumbInfo* inBreadcrumbs)
   450	{
   451	
   452	
   453	    for (auto facet : inheritanceInfo.facets)
   454	    {
   455	        auto containerDeclRef = facet->getDeclRef().as<ContainerDecl>();
   456	        if (!containerDeclRef)
   457	            continue;
   458	
   459	        // Check for cases where we should skip this facet for lookup.
   460	        //
   461	        // If the facet doesn't correspond to a type, we can't lookup.
   462	        if (!facet->getType() || !facet->subtypeWitness)
   463	        {
   464	            continue;
   465	        }
   466	
   467	
   468	        // If we are looking up in an interface, and the lookup request told us
   469	        // to skip interfaces, we should do so here.
   470	        if (auto baseInterfaceDeclRef = containerDeclRef.as<InterfaceDecl>())
   471	        {
   472	            if (int(request.options) & int(LookupOptions::IgnoreBaseInterfaces))
   473	                continue;
   474	        }
   475	        // If we are looking up only immediate members, ignore non "Self" facets or extension to
   476	        // "Self"
   477	        else if (
   478	            int(request.options) & int(LookupOptions::IgnoreInheritance) &&
   479	            (facet.getImpl()->directness != Facet::Directness::Self))
   480	        {
   481	            if (auto extensionDeclRef = facet.getImpl()->getDeclRef().as<ExtensionDecl>())
   482	            {
   483	                if (auto targetType = getTargetType(astBuilder, extensionDeclRef))
   484	                {
   485	                    if (!targetType->equals(selfType))
   486	                    {
   487	                        // If the extension is to the same type as the one we are looking up in, we
   488	                        // should include it in the lookup.
   489	                        continue;
   490	                    }
   491	                }
   492	            }
   493	            else
   494	                continue;
   495	        }
   496	
   497	        // Some things that are syntactically `InheritanceDecl`s don't actually
   498	        // represent a subtype/supertype relationship, and thus we shouldn't
   499	        // include members from the base type when doing lookup in the
   500	        // derived type.

   501	        //
   502	        // TODO: this check currently only works when the facet is a direct
   503	        // basee type of the type we are looking up in. This is OK because the
   504	        // only case where we use `IgnoreForLookupModifier` is for skipping the
   505	        // underlying int type of an enum type. We should either makes this
   506	        // check more general, or just explicitly detect this case here without

   511	            if (inheritanceDeclRef.getDecl()->hasModifier<IgnoreForLookupModifier>())

   518	        BreadcrumbInfo subtypeInfo;
   519	        auto parentDeclRef = facet->declRefForMemberLookup;

   531	            // to create a breadcrumb to track the sub to super indirection.

   552	static void _lookUpMembersInSuperTypeDeclImpl(
   553	    ASTBuilder* astBuilder,
   554	    Name* name,
   555	    DeclRef<Decl> declRef,
   556	    LookupRequest const& request,
   557	    LookupResult& ioResult,
   558	    BreadcrumbInfo* inBreadcrumbs)
   559	{
   560	    auto semantics = request.semantics;
   561	    if (!as<InterfaceDecl>(declRef.getDecl()) &&
   562	        name == astBuilder->getSharedASTBuilder()->getThisTypeName())
   563	    {
   564	        // If we are looking for `This` in anything other than an InterfaceDecl,
   565	        // we just need to return the declRef itself.
   566	        AddToLookupResult(ioResult, CreateLookupResultItem(declRef, inBreadcrumbs));
   567	        return;
   568	    }
   569	
   570	    // If the semantics context hasn't been established yet (e.g. when looking up during parsing),
   571	    // we simply do a direct lookup without considering subtypes or extensions.
   572	    //
   573	    if (!semantics)
   574	    {
   575	        // In this case we can only lookup in an aggregate type.
   576	        if (auto aggTypeDeclBaseRef = declRef.as<AggTypeDeclBase>())
   577	        {
   578	            _lookUpDirectAndTransparentMembers(
   579	                astBuilder,
   580	                name,
   581	                aggTypeDeclBaseRef.getDecl(),
   582	                aggTypeDeclBaseRef,
   583	                request,
   584	                ioResult,
   585	                inBreadcrumbs);
   586	        }
   587	        return;
   588	    }
   589	
   590	    ensureDecl(semantics, declRef.getDecl(), DeclCheckState::ReadyForLookup);
   591	
   592	    // With semantics context, we can do a comprehensive lookup by scanning through
   593	    // the linearized inheritance list.
   594	
   595	    auto selfType = DeclRefType::create(astBuilder, declRef);
   596	    InheritanceInfo inheritanceInfo;
   597	    if (auto extDeclRef = declRef.as<ExtensionDecl>())
   598	    {
   599	        inheritanceInfo = semantics->getShared()->getInheritanceInfo(extDeclRef);
   600	    }

  1000	LookupResult SemanticsVisitor::filterLookupResultByVisibility(const LookupResult& lookupResult)
  1001	{
  1002	    if (!m_outerScope)
  1003	        return lookupResult;
  1004	    LookupResult filteredResult;
  1005	    for (auto item : lookupResult)
  1006	    {
  1007	        if (isDeclVisibleFromScope(item.declRef, m_outerScope))
  1008	            AddToLookupResult(filteredResult, item);
  1009	    }
  1010	    return filteredResult;
  1011	}
  1012	
  1013	LookupResult SemanticsVisitor::filterLookupResultByVisibilityAndDiagnose(
  1014	    const LookupResult& lookupResult,
  1015	    SourceLoc loc,
  1016	    bool& outDiagnosed)
  1017	{
  1018	    outDiagnosed = false;
  1019	    auto result = filterLookupResultByVisibility(lookupResult);
  1020	    if (lookupResult.isValid() && !result.isValid())
  1021	    {
  1022	        getSink()->diagnose(loc, Diagnostics::declIsNotVisible, lookupResult.item.declRef);
  1023	        outDiagnosed = true;
  1024	
  1025	        if (getShared()->isInLanguageServer())
  1026	        {
  1027	            // When in language server mode, return the unfiltered result so we can still
  1028	            // provide language service around it.
  1029	            return lookupResult;
  1030	        }
  1031	    }
  1032	    return result;
  1033	}
  1034	
  1035	bool SemanticsVisitor::isWitnessUncheckedOptional(SubtypeWitness* witness)
  1036	{
  1037	    auto declaredWitness = as<DeclaredSubtypeWitness>(witness);
  1038	    if (!declaredWitness)
  1039	        return false;
  1040	
  1041	    auto decl = declaredWitness->getDeclRef().getDecl();
  1042	    if (!decl || !decl->hasModifier<OptionalConstraintModifier>())
  1043	        return false;
  1044	
  1045	    // Okay, we've found an optional subtype witness. This result needs
  1046	    // to be removed if we're not inside a block that directly checks
  1047	    // if (sub is sup)
  1048	    auto sub = witness->getSub();
  1049	    auto sup = witness->getSup();
  1050	
  1051	    for (auto outerStmtInfo = m_outerStmts; outerStmtInfo; outerStmtInfo = outerStmtInfo->next)
  1052	    {
  1053	        auto outerStmt = outerStmtInfo->stmt;
  1054	        auto ifStmt = as<IfStmt>(outerStmt);
  1055	
  1056	        if (!ifStmt)
  1057	            continue;
  1058	
  1059	        IsTypeExpr* isType = as<IsTypeExpr>(ifStmt->predicate);
  1060	        if (!isType)
  1061	            continue;
  1062	        VarExpr* var = as<VarExpr>(isType->value);
  1063	        if (!var)
  1064	            continue;
  1065	        TypeType* typeType = as<TypeType>(var->type);
  1066	
  1067	        // var->type works for `variable is Interface`, while
  1068	        // typeType->getType() is for `T is Interface`.
  1069	        auto type = typeType ? typeType->getType() : var->type.type;
  1070	        if (type == sub && isType->typeExpr.type == sup)
  1071	        {
  1072	            return false;
  1073	        }
  1074	    }
  1075	
  1076	    // If we got this far, it's both an optional witness and there's no
  1077	    // statement checking its validity.
  1078	    return true;
  1079	}
  1080	
  1081	LookupResult SemanticsVisitor::filterLookupResultByCheckedOptional(const LookupResult& lookupResult)
  1082	{
  1083	    LookupResult filteredResult;
  1084	    for (auto item : lookupResult)
  1085	    {
  1086	        bool optionalConstraintsChecked = true;
  1087	
  1088	        for (auto bb = item.breadcrumbs; bb; bb = bb->next)
  1089	        {
  1090	            auto witness = as<SubtypeWitness>(bb->val);
  1091	            if (!witness)
  1092	                continue;
  1093	
  1094	            if (isWitnessUncheckedOptional(witness))
  1095	            {
  1096	                optionalConstraintsChecked = false;
  1097	                break;
  1098	            }
  1099	        }
  1100

   966	bool SemanticsVisitor::isDeclVisibleFromScope(DeclRef<Decl> declRef, Scope* scope)
   967	{
   968	    auto visibility = getDeclVisibility(declRef.getDecl());
   969	    if (visibility == DeclVisibility::Public)
   970	        return true;
   971	    if (visibility == DeclVisibility::Internal)
   972	    {
   973	        // Check that the decl is in the same module as the scope.
   974	        auto declModule = getModuleDecl(declRef.getDecl());
   975	        if (declModule == getModuleDecl(scope))
   976	            return true;
   977	    }
   978	    if (visibility == DeclVisibility::Private)
   979	    {
   980	        // Check that the decl is in the same or parent container decl as scope.
   981	        Decl* parentContainer = declRef.getDecl();
   982	        for (; parentContainer; parentContainer = parentContainer->parentDecl)
   983	        {
   984	            if (as<AggTypeDeclBase>(parentContainer))
   985	                break;
   986	            if (as<NamespaceDeclBase>(parentContainer))
   987	                break;
   988	        }
   989	
   990	        for (auto s = scope; s; s = s->parent)
   991	        {
   992	            if (s->containerDecl == parentContainer)
   993	                return true;
   994	        }
   995	        return false;
   996	    }
   997	    return false;
   998	}
   999	
  1000	LookupResult SemanticsVisitor::filterLookupResultByVisibility(const LookupResult& lookupResult)

 14624	DeclVisibility getDeclVisibility(Decl* decl)
 14625	{
 14626	    if (as<GenericTypeParamDeclBase>(decl) || as<GenericValueParamDecl>(decl) ||
 14627	        as<GenericTypeConstraintDecl>(decl))
 14628	    {
 14629	        auto genericDecl = as<GenericDecl>(decl->parentDecl);
 14630	        if (!genericDecl)
 14631	            return DeclVisibility::Default;
 14632	        if (genericDecl->inner)
 14633	            return getDeclVisibility(genericDecl->inner);
 14634	        return DeclVisibility::Default;
 14635	    }
 14636	    if (auto genericDecl = as<GenericDecl>(decl))
 14637	        decl = genericDecl->inner;
 14638	    for (; decl; decl = getParentDecl(decl))
 14639	    {
 14640	        if (as<AccessorDecl>(decl))
 14641	            continue;
 14642	        if (as<EnumCaseDecl>(decl))
 14643	            continue;
 14644	        break;
 14645	    }
 14646	    if (!decl)
 14647	        return DeclVisibility::Public;
 14648	
 14649	    for (auto modifier : decl->modifiers)
 14650	    {
 14651	        if (as<PublicModifier>(modifier))
 14652	            return DeclVisibility::Public;
 14653	        else if (as<InternalModifier>(modifier))
 14654	            return DeclVisibility::Internal;
 14655	        else if (as<PrivateModifier>(modifier))
 14656	            return DeclVisibility::Private;
 14657	    }
 14658	    // Interface members will always have the same visibility as the interface itself.
 14659	    if (auto interfaceDecl = findParentInterfaceDecl(decl))
 14660	    {
 14661	        return getDeclVisibility(interfaceDecl);
 14662	    }
 14663	    auto defaultVis = DeclVisibility::Default;
 14664	    if (auto parentModule = getModuleDecl(decl))
 14665	    {
 14666	        defaultVis = parentModule->languageVersion == SLANG_LANGUAGE_VERSION_LEGACY
 14667	                         ? DeclVisibility::Public
 14668	                         : parentModule->defaultVisibility;
 14669	    }
 14670	
 14671	    // Members of other agg type decls will have their default visibility capped to the
 14672	    // parents'.
 14673	    if (as<NamespaceDecl>(decl))
 14674	    {
 14675	        return DeclVisibility::Public;
 14676	    }
 14677	    return defaultVis;
 14678	}

I see - the `staticConstDecl` (LetDecl) is created without any visibility modifier. This means it will get the default visibility, which for non-legacy language version will be `Internal` (module-private). 

So the issue is that when an unscoped enum is marked as `public`, the enum cases themselves get copied to the parent scope as `LetDecl` instances, but those `LetDecl` instances don't inherit the `public` visibility of the enum.

            // create static const decls for each enum case and add them to the container.
            if (auto enumDecl = isUnscopedEnum(decl))
            {
                for (auto enumCase : enumDecl->getMembersOfType<EnumCaseDecl>())
                {
                    auto staticConstDecl = parser->astBuilder->create<LetDecl>();
                    staticConstDecl->nameAndLoc = enumCase->nameAndLoc;
                    addModifier(staticConstDecl, parser->astBuilder->create<HLSLStaticModifier>());
                    addModifier(staticConstDecl, parser->astBuilder->create<ConstModifier>());
                    
                    // Copy visibility modifiers from the enum to the static const decl
                    // so that public unscoped enums have public constants
                    if (auto publicMod = enumDecl->findModifier<PublicModifier>())
                        addModifier(staticConstDecl, parser->astBuilder->create<PublicModifier>());
                    else if (auto internalMod = enumDecl->findModifier<InternalModifier>())
                        addModifier(staticConstDecl, parser->astBuilder->create<InternalModifier>());
                    else if (auto privateMod = enumDecl->findModifier<PrivateModifier>())
                        addModifier(staticConstDecl, parser->astBuilder->create<PrivateModifier>());
                    
                    auto valueExpr = parser->astBuilder->create<VarExpr>();
                    valueExpr->declRef = DeclRef<Decl>(enumCase);
                    staticConstDecl->initExpr = valueExpr;
                    staticConstDecl->loc = enumCase->loc;
                    AddMember(containerDecl, staticConstDecl);
                }
            }'
